treatment "2_condcoop_english-before-keyfixes.ztt"{
	background{
		table globals{

		table DECBEHAV{

			execute = WITHEACH;
		}
		table EARNINGS{
			lifetime = TREATMENT;
			execute = WITHEACH;
		}
		numsubjects = 4;
		numgroups = 2;
		numpracticeperiods = 0;
		numactualperiods = 14;
		exchangerate = 1;
		startendowment = 0;
		showupfee = 0;

		program{
			table = globals;
			do{
				// ==== TREATMENTS ====
				CONDINFO=1; // Full Information on Conditional Strategies
				NOCONDINFO=2; // Information on Actions Only
				
				Treatment=CONDINFO;
				
				
			}
		}
		program{
			table = globals;
			do{
				// ==== PERIOD TYPES ====
				REAL=1;
				TRAINING=2;
				
				
				NumPerTRAINING=4; // Number of Training Periods
				
				// In order to increase comprehension, in first few (in the paper 2 periods) we present the decision stage only before we introduce belief elicitation task. 
				NumPerTRAININGdsonly=2; // Decision Only
				
				NumPerREAL=10; // Number of Real Periods
				
				//===== CONSTANTS =====
				IE=100; // Initial Endowment
				IEg=10;  // Initial Endowment for Beliefs
				cL=0;     
				cM=50;
				cH=100;
				eff=3;  // Efficiency Rate
				
				// Quadratic Scoring Rule Parameters 
				QuadAlpha=20; 
				QuadBeta=20; 
				
				// Increments for the belief sliders
				IncBelief=5;
				
				
				FinalEarningShowUp=3; // EUR 
				ConversionRate=0.05;
				
				//===== Period Display ====
				PeriodType=-1; 
				PeriodNoREAL=-1;
				PeriodNoTRAINING=-1;
				PeriodNoCur=-1;
				
				//===== PAYMENTS =====
				PeriodSelectedAct=-1;
				PeriodSelectedGuess=-1;
				
				//===== TECHNICAL PARAMETERS =====
				RegularTimeOut=-1;
				MovableToNext=-1;
				
				array ComputerDecision[3];
				
				ComputerDecision[1]=cL;
				ComputerDecision[2]=cM;
				ComputerDecision[3]=cH;
				
				
				
				
				
			}
		}
		program{
			table = globals;
			do{
				//===== DEBUG MODE =====
				
				
				//--- TO TURN DEBUG MODE ON ---
				Debug=0; // Set to 1 to enable debug mode
				
				
				//----- Stage Time Parameters----
				DebugTimeOut=-1;
				
				dbgFocusOnStage=0;   // If >0, It will stop only on that stage number
				
				
				//---------------------------------------------
				dbgShouldLeave=-1;
				dbgLeaveAll=-1;
				if (Debug==1) {
				    TimeOut=DebugTimeOut;
				}
				else {
				    TimeOut=RegularTimeOut;
				}
				
				if (Period!=1) {
				    dbgLeaveAll=OLDglobals.find(dbgLeaveAll);
				}
				if (dbgLeaveAll==1) {

				}
				
				dbgCurrentStage=0;
				
				
				
				
				
			}
		}
		program{

				}

				}
				
				
				
				
				
			}

		program{
			table = globals;

				}

				PeriodNoREAL=-1;
				PeriodNoCur=PeriodNoTRAINING;
				MovableSec=4; 
				}
				
				
				
				
				
			}
		}

	stage "IV-Matching"{
		startwaitforall = TRUE;
		singleentry = FALSE;
		singleentrycontinuation = FALSE;
		timeouttype = always;
		timeout = 2;
		program{
			table = subjects;
			do{
				MtchRnd=random();
				
				
				
				
				
				
			}
		}
		program{
			table = subjects;
			do{
				Rank=count(MtchRnd>=:MtchRnd);
				Group=roundup(Rank/2,1);
				FirstPlayer=if(Rank/2<Group,1,0);
				
				
				
				
				
			}
		}
		program{
			table = subjects;
			do{
				tPeriodStart=gettime();
				ConfirmScreen=0;
				WarningScreen=0;
				LeaveStage=0;
				
				
				
				
				
			}
		}
		program{
			table = globals;
			do{
				dbgCurrentStage=dbgCurrentStage+1;
				
				
				// DEBUGGING PROGRAM (Copy/Paste in Every Stage)
				if (Debug==1 & (dbgShouldLeave==1 | (dbgFocusOnStage>0 & dbgFocusOnStage!=dbgCurrentStage))) { 
				subjects.do { 
				Participate=0;
				} 
				}
				
				
				
				
				
			}
		}

			usesbg = TRUE;
			withalertscreen = FALSE;
			noalertscreen = FALSE;

				hasframe = TRUE;

				height = 650p;

					height = 100%;

					}
					item{
						label = "{\\rtf \\fs40 \\qc \\b You will interact with a randomly selected participant }\r\n";
					}
					item{
						label = "<>{\\rtf \\fs32 \\qc \\b Round <PeriodNoCur|1>/<NumPerREAL|1> }";
					}
				}
				standardbox "MatchingTRAINING"{
					hasframe = FALSE;
					width = 100%;
					height = 100%;

					buttonposition = BOTTOMRIGHT;
					buttonsequence = HORIZONTAL;
					item{
						label = "{\\rtf \\fs24 \\qc \\b Please wait }";

	stage "V-BeliefsI"{
		startwaitforall = TRUE;
		singleentry = FALSE;
		singleentrycontinuation = FALSE;
		timeouttype = never;
		timeout = -1;
		program{
			table = globals;
			do{
				dbgCurrentStage=dbgCurrentStage+1;
				
				
				// DEBUGGING PROGRAM (Copy/Paste in Every Stage)
				if (Debug==1 & (dbgShouldLeave==1 | (dbgFocusOnStage>0 & dbgFocusOnStage!=dbgCurrentStage))) { 
				subjects.do { 
				Participate=0;
				} 
				}
				
				
				
				
				
			}
		}
		program{
			table = subjects;
			do{
				tPeriodStart=gettime();
				
				buc_L=0;
				buc_M=0;
				buc_H=0;
				ConfirmQ=0;
				Ebuc_L= QuadAlpha + 2 * QuadBeta  * buc_L * 0.01 - QuadBeta * power(buc_L * 0.01,2)  ;
				Cbuc_L=  QuadBeta * power(buc_L * 0.01,2) ;
				
				Ebuc_M= QuadAlpha + 2 * QuadBeta  * buc_M * 0.01 - QuadBeta * power(buc_M * 0.01,2)  ;
				Cbuc_M=  QuadBeta * power(buc_M * 0.01,2) ;
				
				Ebuc_H= QuadAlpha + 2 * QuadBeta  * buc_H * 0.01 - QuadBeta * power(buc_H * 0.01,2)  ;
				Cbuc_H=  QuadBeta * power(buc_H * 0.01,2) ;
				
				
				
				
				
				
			}
		}
		program{
			table = subjects;
			do{
				if(Period<=NumPerTRAININGdsonly) {
				Participate=0;
				}
				
				
				
				
			}
		}
		screen action{
			usesbg = TRUE;
			withalertscreen = FALSE;
			noalertscreen = FALSE;
			containerbox "Screen Size "{
				hasframe = TRUE;
				width = 1080p;
				height = 600p;
				top = 50p;
				containerbox "TopLabel"{
					hasframe = TRUE;
					width = 100%;
					height = 6%;
					top = 0p;
					standardbox "StageNameTraining"{
						hasframe = TRUE;
						width = 50%;
						height = 100%;
						left = 0p;
						displaycondition = PeriodType==TRAINING;
						buttonposition = BOTTOMRIGHT;
						buttonsequence = HORIZONTAL;
						item{

				tPeriodStart=gettime();
				
				bccL_L=0;
				bccL_M=0;
				bccL_H=0;
				bccM_L=0;
				bccM_M=0;

				EbccL_L= QuadAlpha + 2 * QuadBeta  * bccL_L * 0.01 - QuadBeta * power(bccL_L * 0.01,2)  ;
				CbccL_L=  QuadBeta * power(bccL_L * 0.01,2) ;
				
				EbccL_M= QuadAlpha + 2 * QuadBeta  * bccL_M * 0.01 - QuadBeta * power(bccL_M * 0.01,2)  ;
				CbccL_M=  QuadBeta * power(bccL_M * 0.01,2) ;
				
				EbccL_H= QuadAlpha + 2 * QuadBeta  * bccL_H * 0.01 - QuadBeta * power(bccL_H * 0.01,2)  ;
				CbccL_H=  QuadBeta * power(bccL_H * 0.01,2) ;
				
				//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
				EbccM_L= QuadAlpha + 2 * QuadBeta  * bccM_L * 0.01 - QuadBeta * power(bccM_L * 0.01,2)  ;
				CbccM_L=  QuadBeta * power(bccM_L * 0.01,2) ;
				
				EbccM_M= QuadAlpha + 2 * QuadBeta  * bccM_M * 0.01 - QuadBeta * power(bccM_M * 0.01,2)  ;
				CbccM_M=  QuadBeta * power(bccM_M * 0.01,2) ;
				
				EbccM_H= QuadAlpha + 2 * QuadBeta  * bccM_H * 0.01 - QuadBeta * power(bccM_H * 0.01,2)  ;
				CbccM_H=  QuadBeta * power(bccM_H * 0.01,2) ;
				//----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

	stage "IX-FeedbackAction"{
		startwaitforall = TRUE;
		singleentry = FALSE;
		singleentrycontinuation = FALSE;
		timeouttype = ifnoinput;
		timeout = -1;
		program{
			table = globals;
			do{
				RandBel=roundup(random()*4,1);
				
				
				
				
				
			}
		}
		program{
			table = subjects;
			condition = Period>NumPerTRAINING;
			do{
				//     ..... Getting Opponent Actions ..... ONLY IN REAL STAGES
				opp=find(same(Group) & not(same(Subject)),Subject);
				
				
				ouc=find(Subject==:opp,uc);
				occL=find(Subject==:opp,ccL);
				occM=find(Subject==:opp,ccM);
				occH=find(Subject==:opp,ccH);
				
				if (FirstPlayer==1) {
				    Action=uc;
				
				    if (uc==cL) {
				        oAction= occL;
				    }
				    if (uc==cM) {
				        oAction= occM;
				    }
				    if (uc==cH) {
				        oAction= occH;
				    }
				
				}
				
				if (FirstPlayer==0) {
				    oAction=ouc;
				
				    if (ouc==cL) {
				        Action= ccL;
				    }
				    if (ouc==cM) {
				        Action= ccM;
				    }
				    if (ouc==cH) {
				        Action= ccH;
				    }
				}
				
				// Calculating Earnings from Guessing Task
				            // -----unconditional-----
				if (ouc==cL) {
				    EarningBelief[1]= Ebuc_L - Cbuc_M - Cbuc_H;
				}
				if (ouc==cM) {
				    EarningBelief[1]= Ebuc_M - Cbuc_L - Cbuc_H;
				}
				if (ouc==cH) {
				    EarningBelief[1]= Ebuc_H - Cbuc_L - Cbuc_M;
				}
				           
				
				            // -----conditionalL-----
				
				if (occL==cL) {
				    EarningBelief[2]=EbccL_L - CbccL_M - CbccL_H;
				}
				if (occL==cM) {
				    EarningBelief[2]=EbccL_M - CbccL_L - CbccL_H;
				}
				if (occL==cH) {
				    EarningBelief[2]=EbccL_H - CbccL_L - CbccL_M;
				}
				
				            // -----conditionalM-----
				
				if (occM==cL) {
				    EarningBelief[3]=EbccM_L - CbccM_M - CbccM_H;
				}
				if (occM==cM) {
				    EarningBelief[3]=EbccM_M - CbccM_L - CbccM_H;
				}
				if (occM==cH) {
				    EarningBelief[3]=EbccM_H - CbccM_L - CbccM_M;
				}
				
				
				            // -----conditionalH-----
				if (occH==cL) {
				    EarningBelief[4]=EbccH_L - CbccH_M - CbccH_H;
				}
				if (occH==cM) {
				    EarningBelief[4]=EbccH_M - CbccH_L - CbccH_H;
				}
				if (occH==cH) {
				EarningBelief[4]=EbccH_H - CbccH_L - CbccH_M;
				}
				//----------------------------------------------------------
				
				
				EarningKept=IE-Action;
				EarningReceived=oAction*eff;
				EarningGame=EarningKept + EarningReceived;
				EarningGuess=round(EarningBelief[RandBel],0.01); // Taking a random belief in each stage
				
				
				
				
				
				
			}
		}
		program{
			table = subjects;
			condition = Period<=NumPerTRAINING;
			do{
				//     ..... Getting Opponent Actions ..... ONLY IN COMPUTER STAGES
				opp=-1;
				
				
				ouc=ComputerDecision[roundup(random()*3,1)];
				occL=ComputerDecision[roundup(random()*3,1)];;
				occM=ComputerDecision[roundup(random()*3,1)];;
				occH=ComputerDecision[roundup(random()*3,1)];;
				
				if (FirstPlayer==1) {
				Action=uc;
				
				if (uc==cL) {
				oAction= occL;
				}
				if (uc==cM) {
				oAction= occM;
				}
				if (uc==cH) {
				oAction= occH;
				}
				
				}
				
				if (FirstPlayer==0) {
				    oAction=ouc;
				
				    if (ouc==cL) {
				        Action= ccL;
				    }
				    if (ouc==cM) {
				        Action= ccM;
				    }
				    if (ouc==cH) {
				        Action= ccH;
				    }
				}
				
				EarningKept=IE-Action;
				EarningReceived=oAction*eff;
				EarningGame=EarningKept + EarningReceived;
				
				
				
				
				
				
				
			}
		}
		program{
			table = subjects;
			condition = Period>NumPerTRAINING;
			do{
				// Write Payments to EARNINGS table
				
				EARNINGS.new { 
				    PeriodNoREAL=:PeriodNoREAL;
				    Subject=:Subject;
				    EarningGame=:EarningGame;
				    EarningGuess=:EarningGuess;
				    RandBel=:RandBel;
				}
				
				
				
				
				
			}
		}
		program{
			table = globals;
			do{
				MovableToNext=0;
				later (MovableSec) do {
				MovableToNext=1;
				}
				
				
				
				
				
			}
		}
		program{
			table = globals;
			do{
				dbgCurrentStage=dbgCurrentStage+1;
				
				
				// DEBUGGING PROGRAM (Copy/Paste in Every Stage)
				if (Debug==1 & (dbgShouldLeave==1 | (dbgFocusOnStage>0 & dbgFocusOnStage!=dbgCurrentStage))) { 
				subjects.do { 
				Participate=0;
				} 
				}
				
				
				
				
				
			}
		}
		screen action{
			usesbg = TRUE;
			withalertscreen = FALSE;
			noalertscreen = FALSE;
			containerbox "ScreenSize"{
				hasframe = TRUE;
				width = 1080p;
				height = 600p;
				top = 50p;
				containerbox "TopLabel"{
					hasframe = TRUE;
					width = 100%;
					height = 6%;
					top = 0p;
					standardbox "StageNameTraining"{
						hasframe = TRUE;
						width = 50%;
						height = 100%;
						left = 0p;
						displaycondition = PeriodType==TRAINING;
						buttonposition = BOTTOMRIGHT;
						buttonsequence = HORIZONTAL;
						item{
							label = "{\\rtf \\fs36 \\qc\r\n{\\colortbl;\\red0\\green0\\blue0;\\red255\\green0\\blue0;}\r\n\\b Feedback \\cf2 (Trial Rounds)   }";
						}
					}
					standardbox "StageNameReal"{
						hasframe = TRUE;
						width = 50%;
						height = 100%;
						left = 0p;
						displaycondition = PeriodType==REAL;
						buttonposition = BOTTOMRIGHT;
						buttonsequence = HORIZONTAL;
						item{
							label = "{\\rtf \\fs36 \\qc\r\n{\\colortbl;\\red0\\green0\\blue0;\\red255\\green0\\blue0;}\r\n\\b Feedback\\b0 \\cf2   }";
						}
					}
					standardbox "PeriodNoTraining"{
						hasframe = TRUE;
						width = 50%;
						height = 100%;
						right = 0p;
						displaycondition = PeriodType==TRAINING;
						buttonposition = BOTTOMRIGHT;
						buttonsequence = HORIZONTAL;
						item{
							label = "<>{\\rtf \\fs32 \\qr \\b Round:<PeriodNoCur|1>/<NumPerTRAINING|1> }";
						}
					}
					standardbox "PeriodNoReal"{
						hasframe = TRUE;
						width = 50%;
						height = 100%;
						right = 0p;
						displaycondition = PeriodType==REAL;
						buttonposition = BOTTOMRIGHT;
						buttonsequence = HORIZONTAL;
						item{
							label = "<>{\\rtf \\fs32 \\qr \\b Round:<PeriodNoCur|1>/<NumPerREAL|1> }";
						}
					}
				}
				containerbox "GamePlay"{
					hasframe = FALSE;
					width = 100%;
					height = 50%;
					top = 30%;
					standardbox "FirstPlayerNoCondInfo"{
						hasframe = FALSE;

						item{
							label = "<>{\\rtf \\fs36 \\qc The predetermined response of the other player was to transfer you \\b <oAction|1>  ECU\\b0}";

					standardbox "FirstPlayerCondInfo"{
						hasframe = FALSE;
						width = 100%;

						displaycondition = FirstPlayer==1 & Treatment==CONDINFO;
						buttonposition = BOTTOMRIGHT;
						buttonsequence = HORIZONTAL;
						item{

		screen action{

			containerbox "ScreenSize"{

	stage "XI- Final Feedback"{
		startwaitforall = TRUE;
		singleentry = FALSE;
		singleentrycontinuation = FALSE;
		timeouttype = ifnoinput;
		timeout = -1;
		program{
			table = globals;
			condition = Period==NumPeriods;
			do{
				PeriodSelectedAct=roundup(random()*(NumPeriods-NumPerTRAINING),1);
				PeriodSelectedGuess=roundup(random()*(NumPeriods-NumPerTRAINING),1);
				
				
				
				
				
				
			}
		}
		program{
			table = subjects;
			condition = Period==NumPeriods;
			do{
				FinalEarningGame=EARNINGS.find(Subject==:Subject & PeriodNoREAL==PeriodSelectedAct,EarningGame);
				FinalEarningGuess=EARNINGS.find(Subject==:Subject & PeriodNoREAL==PeriodSelectedGuess,EarningGuess);
				DecisionSelected=EARNINGS.find(Subject==:Subject & PeriodNoREAL==PeriodSelectedGuess,RandBel);
				FinalMoney=(FinalEarningGame + FinalEarningGuess) * ConversionRate + FinalEarningShowUp;
				FinalMoney=roundup(FinalMoney,0.01);
				
				
				
				
				
				
				
			}
		}
		program{
			table = subjects;
			condition = Period==NumPeriods;
			do{
				session.do {
				    if (Subject==:Subject) {
				        FinalProfit=:FinalMoney;
				        ShowUpFee=0;
				     }
				}
				
				
				
				
				
			}
		}
		program{
			table = subjects;
			do{
				Participate=if(Period==NumPeriods,1,0);
				
				
				
				
				
			}
		}
		program{
			table = globals;
			do{
				dbgCurrentStage=dbgCurrentStage+1;
				
				
				// DEBUGGING PROGRAM (Copy/Paste in Every Stage)
				if (Debug==1 & (dbgShouldLeave==1 | (dbgFocusOnStage>0 & dbgFocusOnStage!=dbgCurrentStage))) { 
				subjects.do { 
				Participate=0;
				} 
				}
				
				
				
				
				
			}
		}
		screen action{
			usesbg = TRUE;
			withalertscreen = FALSE;
			noalertscreen = FALSE;
			containerbox "ScreenSize"{
				hasframe = TRUE;
				width = 800p;
				height = 650p;
				containerbox "GamePlay"{
					hasframe = FALSE;
					width = 100%;
					height = 50%;
					top = 30%;
					standardbox "Standard"{
						hasframe = FALSE;
						width = 100%;
						height = 100%;
						buttonposition = BOTTOMRIGHT;
						buttonsequence = HORIZONTAL;
						item{
							label = "<>{\\rtf \\fs36 \\qc \\ul \\b Summary }";
						}
						item{
							label = "<>{\\rtf \\fs28 \\ql Payment for the participation(EUR): <FinalEarningShowUp|.01> }\r\n\r\n";
						}
						item{
						}
						item{
							label = "<>{\\rtf \\fs28 \\ql Round selected for the decision stage \\b0: <PeriodSelectedAct|1> }\r\n\r\n";
						}
						item{
							label = "<>{\\rtf \\fs28 \\ql ECU obtained in the \\b decision stage \\b0: <FinalEarningGame|1> }\r\n\r\n";
						}
						item{
							label = "<>{\\rtf \\fs28 \\ql Value in EUROS \\b0: <FinalEarningGame* ConversionRate|.01> }\r\n\r\n";
						}
						item{
						}
						item{
						}
						item{
							label = "<>{\\rtf \\fs28 \\ql Round selected for the expectations stage \\b0: <PeriodSelectedGuess|1> }\r\n\r\n";
						}
						item{
							label = "<>{\\rtf \\fs28 \\ql Other player's decision at the \\b expectations round \\b0: <DecisionSelected|!text: 1=\"As player 1\"; 2=\"As player 2, response to the transfer of 0\"; 3=\"As player 2, response to the transfer of 50\"; 4=\"As player 2, response to the transfer of 100;\"> }\r\n\r\n";
						}
						item{
							label = "<>{\\rtf \\fs28 \\ql ECU obtained in the \\b expectations stage \\b0: <FinalEarningGuess|.01> }\r\n\r\n";
						}
						item{
							label = "<>{\\rtf \\fs28 \\ql Value in EUROS \\b0: <FinalEarningGuess* ConversionRate|.01> }\r\n\r\n";
						}
						item{
						}
						item{
							label = "<>{\\rtf \\fs36 \\ql \\b Total earnings in the experiment (EUR): <FinalMoney|.01> \\b0 }\r\n\r\n";
						}
					}
				}
				containerbox "Confirmation"{
					hasframe = FALSE;
					width = 50%;
					height = 10%;
					bottom = 0p;
					standardbox "Confirma"{
						hasframe = FALSE;
						width = 100%;
						height = 100%;
						buttonposition = BOTTOMRIGHT;
						buttonsequence = HORIZONTAL;
						item{
							label = "To continue click on \"Continue\".";
						}
						button "Continue"{
							clearinputafterok = FALSE;
							norecordmadeorselected = FALSE;
							terminatestage = TRUE;
							donotterminatestage = FALSE;
							specialbuttoncolor = TRUE;
							buttoncolor = 5921535;
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		screen wait{
			usesbg = TRUE;
			withalertscreen = FALSE;
			noalertscreen = FALSE;
		}
	}
